    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

  <span id="freeText9617739982439930917" style="display:none">What had happened to the ever so confident Dhani? Why wasn’t she sure of herself anymore? She wondered if she would be the same Dhani ever again. <br />Dhani, a girl who thought her life was finally perfect, was now seeing it fall apart. But she was too proud to accept in front of the world about how defeated she felt.<br /><br /> Dhruv had braved every hurdle that life had thrown at him; and when he finally felt complete with Dhani by his side, destiny showed him its ugliest face ever. <br /><br />Embark on a journey of love in its purest form. Love between a father and daughter, a brother and sister, a man and woman; and the love above any other… love for one's motherland, and the urge to protect it at any cost. <br /><br />Diya Aur Baati Hum tells us the story of a love so potent, it changes lives and destinies. A beautiful story of love, friendship, faith, acceptance, hope and courage.</span>

The story takes you from a love triangle to a full romance and then the thrill of what is going to happen next keeps you on your toes. I love the way relations are portrayed in the story, they are strong and caring. <br/>I especially like the army part of the movie and the way the author connects the threads.<br/><br/>It's a must read for a person who loves romance but with a ting of thriller.<br/><br/>Would like to read a thriller from the author, since I got a glimpse of it</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer681230952453487372">Diya aur Bati hum.. this name may sound traditional but the story, the connection, bond, characters are way beyond amazing.. word can not justify this love, friendship and thriller saga.. what a beautiful way emotions, relationships and suspense have been weaved in the storyline.. this book deserves a read .. it’s a book for keeps and to cherish forever❤️Go take a dive in this beautiful amazing world of Dhruv and Dhani </span>

          </span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8112388050229682181">Book - Diya Aur Baati Hum<br/>Author - Snehlata Agarwala<br/>Rating - ⭐⭐⭐⭐/5<br/>"Diya Aur Baati Hum" by Snehlata Agarwala is a worth reading story of Dhani.<br/>To be honest, the book is one of the finest stories that I have read so far.<br/><br/>The book contains emotions such as the pain of losing someone you truly love, immense pain, separation, motherhood and will to live again.<br/>🪔<br/>"Diya Aur Baati Hum" revolves around the life of Dhani, who is a confident girl and thinks her life is so perfect, but nobody's life is perfect</span>
  <span id="freeText8112388050229682181" style="display:none">Book - Diya Aur Baati Hum<br />Author - Snehlata Agarwala<br />Rating - ⭐⭐⭐⭐/5<br />"Diya Aur Baati Hum" by Snehlata Agarwala is a worth reading story of Dhani.<br />To be honest, the book is one of the finest stories that I have read so far.<br /><br />The book contains emotions such as the pain of losing someone you truly love, immense pain, separation, motherhood and will to live again.<br />🪔<br />"Diya Aur Baati Hum" revolves around the life of Dhani, who is a confident girl and thinks her life is so perfect, but nobody's life is perfect, right?<br />Then there's Dhruv.<br />Dhani's admirer, lover, soulmate...<br /><br />Both Dhani and Dhruv love each other unconditionally.<br />They are made for each other and they live happily together.<br />Then destiny challenges Dhani and plays its card, breaking her completely...<br />🪔<br />The book is an emotional read which takes the readers on a journey of love in its purest and sincerest form.<br />The bond between a father and daughter, love between a couple, and relationship of a brother and sister are beautifully shown through the story.<br />🪔<br />"Diya Aur Baati Hum" is a long read but it didn't bore me at all. It kept me glued to my seat the entire time.<br /><br />The plot sends a beautiful message to the readers- to dream again, to love again, to let go past and to smile again. Not a pretentious smile but a real one!!<br />🪔<br />I very much enjoyed the storyline of the book. The cover is so beautiful and the title looks promising.<br /><br />All the incidents and characters are well described.<br />Kudos to the author.<br />Can't wait to read more of her books...<br />#diyaaurbaatihum #snehlataagarwala #readingisgood #amazon #instagram #goodreads #kindle #facebook #review #readnovels #ebook #paperback #pratibhamalav #misswriter #author #reviewer #influencer #writersofinstagram #reviewersofinstagram #indianreviewer #readbooks #staybusy #stayhappy #ilovemyself #cheers</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('GQCKDxV6+8aw9aq2ZUa5ZHbVqy5HbzdOpdtkd1DWn6Y39jJz05NzTK69aX2uGQKqvb+wF/l8yD8mZOkZGDxRMQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('2Y8OiqssjpouOCONuOXkt5/LpD0agMeSweifp0PPmqb3ebb2bcUGEDBw4EZzul95VKG/BKSTOONCVxLJCyVUMQ==')})
  }
